## TCGA_VERSIONED.SOMATIC_MUTATION_HG19_MC3_2017_02
Codons: TEXT | Alternative codons with the variant base in upper case
AA_MAF: TEXT | Non-reference allele and frequency of existing variant in NHLBI-ESP African American population
Tumor_Seq_Allele1: TEXT | Primary data genotype for tumor sequencing (discovery) allele 1. A - symbol for a deletion represents a variant. A - symbol for an insertion represents wild-type allele. Novel inserted sequence for insertion does not include flanking reference bases
CANONICAL: TEXT | A flag (YES) indicating that the VEP-based canonical transcript, the longest translation, was used for this gene, if not, the value is null
dbSNP_RS: TEXT | Rs-IDs from the dbSNP database, novel if not found in any database used, or null if there is no dbSNP record, but it is found in other databases
PUBMED: TEXT | Pubmed ID(s) of publications that cite existing variant
project_short_name: TEXT | Project name abbreviation; the program name appended with a project name abbreviation; eg. TCGA-OV, etc.
CLIN_SIG: TEXT | Clinical significance of variant from dbSNP
SOMATIC: TEXT | Somatic status of each ID reported under Existing_variation (0, 1, or null)
SWISSPROT: TEXT | UniProtKB/Swiss-Prot accession
Existing_variation: TEXT | Known identifier of existing variation
Variant_Classification: TEXT | Translational effect of variant allele
AMR_MAF: TEXT | Non-reference allele and frequency of existing variant in 1000 Genomes combined American population
STRAND: NUMBER | DNA strand (1 or -1) on which the transcript/feature lies
FILTER: TEXT | Copied from input VCF. This includes filters implemented directly by the variant caller and other external software used in the DNA-Seq pipeline
VARIANT_CLASS: TEXT | Sequence Ontology variant class
Tumor_Seq_Allele2: TEXT | Primary data genotype for tumor sequencing (discovery) allele 2. A - symbol for a deletion represents a variant. A - symbol for an insertion represents wild-type allele. Novel inserted sequence for insertion does not include flanking reference bases
HGVSp: TEXT | Protein sequence of the variant in HGVS recommended format. p.= signifies no change in the protein
CCDS: TEXT | CCDS identifier for this transcript, where applicable
INTRON: TEXT | Intron number (out of total number)
End_Position: NUMBER | End position, in 1-based integer coordinates
Protein_position: TEXT | Relative position of affected amino acid in protein. A - symbol is displayed as the numerator if the variant does not appear in coding sequence
EXON: TEXT | Exon number (out of total number)
Transcript_ID: TEXT | Ensembl ID of the transcript affected by the variant
Start_Position: NUMBER | Lowest numeric position of the reported variant on the genomic reference sequence. Mutation start coordinate
n_alt_count: NUMBER | Read depth supporting the variant allele in normal BAM (cleared in somatic MAF)
Feature: TEXT | Stable Ensembl ID of feature (transcript, regulatory, motif)
UNIPARC: TEXT | UniParc identifier of protein product
DBVS: TEXT | |-delimited list eg byCluster|by1000G
TREMBL: TEXT | UniProtKB/TrEMBL identifier of protein product
GMAF: TEXT | Non-reference allele and frequency of existing variant in 1000 Genomes
Amino_acids: TEXT | Amino acid substitution caused by the mutation, only given if the variation affects the protein-coding sequence
EA_MAF: TEXT | Non-reference allele and frequency of existing variant in NHLBI-ESP European American population
Consequence: TEXT | Consequence type of this variant; sequence ontology terms
case_barcode: TEXT | Original TCGA case barcode, eg TCGA-12-1089  --  note that each case typically has a primary-tumor sample and a matched-normal (blood or adjacent tissue) sample; please refer to the TCGA Biospecimen table for more details
CDS_position: TEXT | Relative position of base pair in coding sequence. A - symbol is displayed as the numerator if the variant does not appear in coding sequence
cDNA_position: TEXT | Relative position of base pair in the cDNA sequence as a fraction. A - symbol is displayed as the numerator if the variant does not appear in cDNA
all_effects: TEXT | A semicolon delimited list of all possible variant effects, sorted by priority ([Symbol,Consequence,HGVSp_Short,Transcript_ID,RefSeq,HGVSc,Impact,Canonical,Sift,PolyPhen,Strand])
Exon_Number: TEXT | Exon number (out of total number)
EUR_MAF: TEXT | Non-reference allele and frequency of existing variant in 1000 Genomes combined European population
Feature_type: TEXT | Type of feature. Currently one of Transcript, RegulatoryFeature, MotifFeature (or blank)
HGVSc: TEXT | Coding sequence of the variant in HGVS recommended format
t_ref_count: NUMBER | Read depth supporting the reference allele in tumor BAM
AFR_MAF: TEXT | Non-reference allele and frequency of existing variant in 1000 Genomes combined African population
Variant_Type: TEXT | Type of mutation. TNP (tri-nucleotide polymorphism) is analogous to DNP (di-nucleotide polymorphism) but for three consecutive nucleotides. ONP (oligo-nucleotide polymorphism) is analogous to TNP but for consecutive runs of four or more (SNP, DNP, TNP, ONP, INS, DEL, or Consolidated)
EAS_MAF: TEXT | Non-reference allele and frequency of existing variant in 1000 Genomes combined East Asian population
Hugo_Symbol: TEXT | HUGO symbol for the gene (HUGO symbols are always in all caps). Unknown is used for regions that do not correspond to a gene
aliquot_barcode_normal: TEXT | TCGA aliquot barcode for the normal control, eg TCGA-12-1089-01A-01D-0517-01
n_ref_count: NUMBER | Read depth supporting the reference allele in normal BAM (cleared in somatic MAF)
IMPACT: TEXT | Impact modifier for the consequence type
sample_barcode_normal: TEXT | TCGA sample barcode for the normal control, eg TCGA-12-1089-01A. One sample may have multiple sets of CN segmentations corresponding to multiple aliquots; use GROUP BY appropriately in queries
SIFT: TEXT | SIFT prediction and/or score, with both given as prediction (score)
Gene: TEXT | The gene symbol. In this table, gene symbol is simulated data e.g. ENSG00000251562
PolyPhen: TEXT | PolyPhen prediction and/or score
SYMBOL_SOURCE: TEXT | The source of the gene symbol, usually HGNC, rarely blank, other sources include Uniprot_gn, EntrezGene, etc
NCALLERS: NUMBER | Number of callers: a value between 2 and 8 (most common is 5)
HGVS_OFFSET: NUMBER | Indicates by how many bases the HGVS notations for this variant have been shifted
t_alt_count: NUMBER | Read depth supporting the variant allele in tumor BAM
aliquot_barcode_tumor: TEXT | TCGA aliquot barcode for the tumor, eg TCGA-12-1089-01A-01D-0517-01
DOMAINS: TEXT | Source and identifier of any overlapping protein domains
PHENO: TEXT | Indicates if existing variant is associated with a phenotype, disease or trait (0, 1, or null)
COSMIC: TEXT | Overlapping COSMIC variants
HGNC_ID: NUMBER | Gene identifier from the HUGO Gene Nomenclature Committee if applicable
DISTANCE: NUMBER | Shortest distance from the variant to transcript
BIOTYPE: TEXT | Biotype of transcript
ENSP: TEXT | Ensembl protein identifier of the affected transcript
HGVSp_Short: TEXT | Same as the HGVSp column, but using 1-letter amino-acid codes
CONTEXT: TEXT | Reference allele per VCF specs, and its five flanking base pairs
ASN_MAF: TEXT | Non-reference allele and frequency of existing variant in 1000 Genomes combined Asian population
n_depth: NUMBER | Read depth across this locus in normal BAM
SAS_MAF: TEXT | Non-reference allele and frequency of existing variant in 1000 Genomes combined South Asian population
t_depth: NUMBER | Read depth across this locus in tumor BAM
Reference_Allele: TEXT | The plus strand reference allele at this position. Includes the deleted sequence for a deletion or - for an insertion
SYMBOL: TEXT | Eg TP53, LRP1B, etc (same as Hugo_Symbol field except blank instead of Unknown
Chromosome: TEXT | Chromosome, possible values: 1, X, etc (ie does not include chr prefix)
NCBI_Build: TEXT | The reference genome used for the alignment (GRCh37)
sample_barcode_tumor: TEXT | TCGA sample barcode for the tumor, eg TCGA-12-1089-01A. One sample may have multiple sets of CN segmentations corresponding to multiple aliquots; use GROUP BY appropriately in queries
CALLERS: TEXT | |-delimited list of mutation caller(s) that agreed on this particular call, always in alphabetical order: muse, mutect, somaticsniper, varscan

## TCGA_VERSIONED.MIRNASEQ_ISOFORM_HG38_GDC_R14
mirna_transcript: TEXT | The type of transcript -- either mature, precursor, unannotated, or stemloop  (if this value is not mature, then the mirna_accession field will be null)
cross_mapped: TEXT | A short isomiR read may map exactly to mature strands whose sequences are similar but not identical, when the read sequence does not capture the bases that distinguish these miRNAs (e.g. hsa-mir-30a at 6q13 and hsa-mir-30e at 1p34.2, which differ at position 18). We report such a <line_feed> read as cross-mapped, and we increment the read count for each MIMAT that it mapped to. Either Y or N -- fewer than 2% are Y
end_pos: NUMBER | 1-based end chromosome position of isoform
strand: TEXT | Either + or - to denote whether read mapped to the sense (+) or anti-sense (-) strand
mirna_id: TEXT | Unique miRNA id (aka symbol), eg hsa-mir-21  --  relevant reference information can be found in the isb-cgc:genome_reference dataset in the tables miRBase_v21 and miRBase_v21_hsa_gff4
aliquot_barcode: TEXT | TCGA aliquot barcode, eg TCGA-12-1089-01A-01D-0517-29
sample_barcode: TEXT | TCGA sample barcode, eg TCGA-12-1089-01A. One sample may have multiple sets of CN segmentations corresponding to multiple aliquots; use GROUP BY appropriately in queries
mirna_accession: TEXT | The mature miRNA accession id (eg MIMAT0000062) -- note that this can also be null, in the event that this read does not map to a mature portion of the miRNA
project_short_name: TEXT | Project name abbreviation; the program name appended with a project name abbreviation; eg. TCGA-OV, etc.
read_count: NUMBER | Number of reads that were mapped to this mirna_id
reads_per_million_miRNA_mapped: FLOAT | Read count normalized by total reads mapped divided by 1 million
start_pos: NUMBER | 1-based start chromosome position of isoform
chromosome: TEXT | Chromosome, possible values: chr1-22, and chrX
case_barcode: TEXT | Original TCGA case barcode, eg TCGA-DX-A8BN

sample_barcode: TEXT | Original TCGA sample barcode, eg TCGA-12-1089-01A  --  note that one sample may have multiple aliquots and therefore multiple sets of CN segmentations; so be sure to use GROUP BY appropriately in your queries
project_short_name: TEXT | Project name abbreviation; the program name appended with a project name abbreviation; eg. TCGA-OV, etc.
beta_value: FLOAT | Normalized DNA methylation beta value (between 0 and 1, where 0 indicates completely un-methylated and 1 indicates fully methylated)

## TCGA_VERSIONED.COPY_NUMBER_GENE_LEVEL_HG38_GDC_R36
copy_number: NUMBER | The weighted median of the strand copy numbers. Gene-level copy number data is generated by intersection of copy number segment and gene ranges. It is possible for one gene to overlap with multiple segments, and in this case, copy_number, min_copy_number and max_copy_number could take different values. In particular, the copy_number value is calculated as the median, weighted on length of overlapped bases, of segment copy numbers from all overlapped segments.
primary_site: TEXT | Anatomical site of the cancer under investigation or review
gene_type: TEXT | The type of genetic element the reads mapped to, eg. protein_coding, ribozyme
sample_gdc_id: TEXT | Unique GDC identifier for this sample (corresponds to the sample_barcode), eg a1ec9279-c1a6-4e58-97ed-9ec1f36187c5  --  this can be used to access more information from the GDC data portal
end_pos: NUMBER | 1-based end chromosome position of isoform
start_pos: NUMBER | 1-based start chromosome position of isoform
gene_name: TEXT | Gene name eg. TTN, DDR1

Tumor_Seq_Allele1: TEXT | Primary data genotype for tumor sequencing (discovery) allele 1. A - symbol for a deletion represents a variant. A - symbol for an insertion represents wild-type allele. Novel inserted sequence for insertion does not include flanking reference bases
TRANSCRIPTION_FACTORS: TEXT | List of transcription factors which bind to the transcription factor binding profile
Verification_Status: TEXT | Second pass results from independent attempt using same methods as primary data source. Generally reserved for 3730 Sanger Sequencing
Match_Norm_Validation_Allele1: TEXT | Secondary data from orthogonal technology. Matched normal genotyping (validation) for allele 1. A - symbol for a deletion represents a variant. A - symbol for an insertion represents wild-type allele. Novel inserted sequence for insertion does not include flanking reference bases (cleared in somatic MAF)
gnomAD_non_cancer_FIN_AF: FLOAT | Frequency of exisiting variant in gnomAD genomes non-cancer Finnish population
gnomAD_AF: FLOAT | Frequency of existing variant in gnomAD exomes combined population
Sequencing_Phase: TEXT | TCGA sequencing phase (if applicable). Phase should change under any circumstance that the targets under consideration change
Feature_type: TEXT | Type of feature. Currently one of Transcript, RegulatoryFeature, MotifFeature (or blank)
aliquot_barcode_normal: TEXT | TCGA aliquot barcode for the normal control, eg TCGA-12-1089-01A-01D-0517-01]
APPRIS: TEXT | Annotates alternatively spliced transcripts as primary or alternate based on a range of computational methods
One_Consequence: TEXT | The single consequence of the canonical transcript in  sequence ontology terms, eg missense_variant
ThousG_AMR_AF: FLOAT | Non-reference allele and frequency of existing variant in 1000 Genomes combined American population
Mutation_Status: TEXT | An assessment of the mutation as somatic, germline, LOH, post transcriptional modification, unknown, or none. The values allowed in this field are constrained by the value in the Validation_Status field
Score: TEXT | Not in use
Allele: TEXT | The variant allele used to calculate the consequence
callers: TEXT | |-delimited list of mutation caller(s) that agreed on this particular call, always in alphabetical order: muse, mutect, somaticsniper, varscan
n_depth: NUMBER | Read depth across this locus in normal BAM
DISTANCE: TEXT | Shortest distance from the variant to transcript
gnomAD_non_cancer_EAS_AF: FLOAT | Frequency of exisiting variant in gnomAD genomes non-cancer East Asian population
HGVSp_Short: TEXT | Same as the HGVSp column, but using 1-letter amino-acid codes
Tumor_Validation_Allele1: TEXT | Secondary data from orthogonal technology. Tumor genotyping (validation) for allele 1. A - symbol for a deletion represents a variant. A - symbol for an insertion represents wild-type allele. Novel inserted sequence for insertion does not include flanking reference bases
gnomAD_non_cancer_OTH_AF: FLOAT | Frequency of exisiting variant in gnomAD genomes non-cancer Other population
sample_barcode_normal: TEXT | TCGA sample barcode for the normal control, eg TCGA-12-1089-01A. One sample may have multiple sets of CN segmentations corresponding to multiple aliquots; use GROUP BY appropriately in queries
case_id: TEXT | Unique GDC identifier for the underlying case
dbSNP_Val_Status: TEXT | The dbSNP validation status is reported as a semicolon-separated list of statuses. The union of all rs-IDs is taken when there are multiple

ThousG_EAS_AF: FLOAT | Non-reference allele and frequency of existing variant in 1000 Genomes combined East Asian population
ThousG_AFR_AF: FLOAT | Non-reference allele and frequency of existing variant in 1000 Genomes combined African population
project_short_name: TEXT | Project name abbreviation; the program name appended with a project name abbreviation; eg. TCGA-OV, etc.
gnomAD_non_cancer_ASJ_AF: FLOAT | Frequency of exisiting variant in gnomAD genomes non-cancer Ashkenazi Jewish population
Protein_position: TEXT | Relative position of affected amino acid in protein. A - symbol is displayed as the numerator if the variant does not appear in coding sequence
file_gdc_id: TEXT | |-delimited list of unique GDC identifiers for underlying MAF file
RNA_depth: TEXT | Read depth at this locus if the variant is supported by tumor RNA-seq data.
MOTIF_NAME: TEXT | The source and identifier of a transcription factor binding profile aligned at this position
MAX_AF_POPS: TEXT | Populations in which maximum allele frequency was observed
SYMBOL_SOURCE: TEXT | The source of the gene symbol, usually HGNC, rarely blank, other sources include Uniprot_gn, EntrezGene, etc
Transcript_ID: TEXT | Ensembl ID of the transcript affected by the variant
HIGH_INF_POS: TEXT | A flag indicating if the variant falls in a high information position of a transcription factor binding profile (TFBP) (Y, N, or null)
gnomAD_AFR_AF: FLOAT | Frequency of existing variant in gnomAD exomes African/American population
RNA_Support: TEXT | Indicates if the variant is found and alleles (Match), simply (Overlap), or is not supported (No) by tumor RNA-Seq. If it has not been checked against RNA-Seq data, the value will be 'Unknown'.
Chromosome: TEXT | Chromosome, possible values: chr1-22, and chrX
aliquot_barcode_tumor: TEXT | TCGA aliquot barcode for the tumor, eg TCGA-12-1089-01A-01D-0517-01
gnomAD_non_cancer_AF: FLOAT | Frequency of exisiting variant in gnomAD genomes combined non-cancer population
PolyPhen: TEXT | The PolyPhen prediction and/or score
RefSeq: TEXT | RefSeq identifier for this transcript
gnomAD_non_cancer_AMR_AF: FLOAT | Frequency of exisiting variant in gnomAD genomes non-cancer Latino population
IMPACT: TEXT | The impact modifier for the consequence type
Match_Norm_Seq_Allele2: TEXT | Matched normal sequencing allele 2
mutect2: TEXT | Mutect2 caller identified the variant at this position
Hugo_Symbol: TEXT | HUGO symbol for the gene (HUGO symbols are always in all caps). Unknown is used for regions that do not correspond to a gene
Amino_acids: TEXT | Amino acid substitution caused by the mutation. Only given if the variation affects the protein-coding sequence
gnomAD_non_cancer_NFE_AF: FLOAT | Frequency of exisiting variant in gnomAD genomes non-cancer Non-Finnish European population
muse: TEXT | Muse caller identified the variant at this position
gnomAD_non_cancer_MAX_AF_adj: FLOAT | Maximum observed allele frequency in non-cancer gnomAD genomes populations after removing subpopulations with less than 2 allele counts
PICK: TEXT | Indicates if this block of consequence data was picked by VEP's   pick feature (1 or null)
ENSP: TEXT | The Ensembl protein identifier of the affected transcript
BAM_File: TEXT | Not in use
MAX_AF: FLOAT | Maximum observed allele frequency in 1000 Genomes, ESP and ExAC/gnomAD
UNIPROT_ISOFORM: TEXT | Direct mappings to UniProtKB isoforms
Gene: TEXT | The gene symbol. In this table, gene symbol is gene name e.g. ACADVL
NCBI_Build: TEXT | The reference genome used for the alignment (GRCh38)
SIFT: TEXT | The SIFT prediction and/or score, with both given as prediction (score)
dbSNP_RS: TEXT | The rs-IDs from the   dbSNP database, novel if not found in any database used, or null if there is no dbSNP record, but it is found in other databases
ESP_EA_AF: FLOAT | Non-reference allele and frequency of existing variant in NHLBI-ESP European American population
normal_submitter_uuid: TEXT | Unique GDC identifier for the normal file submitter
End_Position: NUMBER | Highest numeric genomic position of the reported variant on the genomic reference sequence. Mutation end coordinate
HGVSp: TEXT | The protein sequence of the variant in HGVS recommended format. p.= signifies no change in the protein
TSL: TEXT | Transcript support level, which is based on independent RNA analyses
FLAGS: TEXT | Transcript quality flags
Tumor_Aliquot_Barcode: TEXT | Aliquot barcode for the tumor sample
n_ref_count: TEXT | Read depth supporting the reference allele in normal BAM (cleared in somatic MAF)
Exon_Number: TEXT | The exon number (out of total number)
GENE_PHENO: TEXT | Indicates if gene that the variant maps to is associated with a phenotype, disease or trait (0, 1, or null)

SpacingBetweenSlices: FLOAT | Spacing Between Slices. DICOM has an attribute called Spacing Between Slices (0018, 0088) that gives the distance between two adjacent slices (perpendicular to the image plane) and it also has an attribute called Slice Thickness (0018, 0050) that gives the thickness of the imaged slice (the image plane exists at the center of the slice, with half of the volume above the plane and half below). Image Position (Patient) (0020, 0032) and Image Orientation (Patient) (0020, 0037) are also useful attributes for computing spatial relationships between slices. For a more detailed explanation, see section C.7.6.2 of part 3 of the DICOM standard. (p. 409) WARNING: Please be aware that different vendors use the same dicom tags for addressing different things. Examples: 5.0, 6.0, 10.0, 15.0. 40.0. See https://www.materialise.com/en/faq/what-difference-between-slice-thickness-and-slice-increment
PerformedProcedureStepDescription: TEXT | Performed Procedure Step Description. Examples: MRI BRAIN W/ENHANCEMENT, IC MRI ABD WO+W CON
PatientAge: NUMBER | Patient Age. Examples: 52, 60, 65, 70 (or null)
DCMFileName: TEXT | DCM FileName. Examples: 058.dcm, 273.dcm, 1203.dcm, 093.dcm
ProtocolName: TEXT | Protocol Name. Examples: TVP EXCITE SURGICAL/9, TVP Surgical/, ROUTINE BRAIN/
StudyInstanceUID: TEXT | StudyInstanceUID. Example: 1.3.6.1.4.1.14519.5.2.1.7695.4001.163028456110647174493384721797
ContentTime: FLOAT | Content Time. Example: 100545.0
SeriesInstanceUID: TEXT | Series Instance UID. Example: 1.2.826.0.1.3680043.2.1322.2.2837147000.102512129439.0
Rows: NUMBER | Rows. Example: 128
SeriesNumber: NUMBER | Series Number. Examples: 800, 501, 15, 362
AdditionalPatientHistory: TEXT | Additional Patient History. Examples: RENAL MASSCIRROHIS1A, BRAIN LAB, liver lesion
SpacingBetweenSlices: FLOAT | Spacing Between Slices. DICOM has an attribute called Spacing Between Slices (0018, 0088) that gives the distance between two adjacent slices (perpendicular to the image plane) and it also has an attribute called Slice Thickness (0018, 0050) that gives the thickness of the imaged slice (the image plane exists at the center of the slice, with half of the volume above the plane and half below). Image Position (Patient) (0020, 0032) and Image Orientation (Patient) (0020, 0037) are also useful attributes for computing spatial relationships between slices. For a more detailed explanation, see section C.7.6.2 of part 3 of the DICOM standard. (p. 409) WARNING: Please be aware that different vendors use the same dicom tags for addressing different things. For instance, the attribute Spacing Between Slices (0018, 0088) means two different things depending on the vendor.Examples: 4.5, 6.0, 7.5, 12.0. 69.2, 5.1
SOPClassUID: TEXT | SOP Class UID. Examples: MR Image Storage, Nuclear Medicine Image Storage, Positron Emission Tomography Image Storage, CT Image Storage, Digital Mammography X-Ray Image Storage - For Processing
Modality: TEXT | Modality. Examples: MR, DT, PT, OT, CTPT, DX, NM
PixelRepresentation: NUMBER | Pixel Representation. Either 0 or 1
MRAcquisitionType: TEXT | MR Acquisition Type.Either 2D or 3D (or null)

SOPInstanceUID: TEXT | SOP Instance UID. Example: 1.3.6.1.4.1.14519.5.2.1.6450.4007.621199411198673382052605519396
SeriesTime: FLOAT | Series Time. Examples: 92042.0, 121428.0. (may be null)
StudyDate: NUMBER | Study Date. Example: 20001225
ReconstructionDiameter: FLOAT | Reconstruction Diameter. Examples: 160.0, 222.0, 500.0, 700.00 (may be null)
ZipFileName: TEXT | Zip File Name. Example: gs://isb-tcia-open/images/TCGA-GBM/TCGA-06-0137/TCIA.image.1.2.826.0.1.3680043.2.1322.2.2834599022.102511191651.0.zip
PatientID: TEXT | Patient ID. Example: TCGA-08-0352
